class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 eRvpKx"><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 cTsUqU js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Awesome CF Generation</h1><a id="user-content-awesome-cf-generation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Awesome CF Generation" href="#awesome-cf-generation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This repository contains the frontier research on counterfactual generation which is a hot topic recently.  A counterfactual is obtained by making minimal or loose changes to existing data to flip their label for a particular NLP task. The counterfactually augmented data (CAD) consists of original data and counterfactuals, also called contrast sets (Gardner et al., 2020; Atanasova et al., 2022).</p>
<p dir="auto">Here are some examples of counterfactuals based on sentiment analysis and natural language inference tasks.</p>
 <p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Siki-cloud/Awesome-CF-Generation/blob/main/image/cfs_example.png"><img src="/Siki-cloud/Awesome-CF-Generation/raw/main/image/cfs_example.png" width="70%" alt="Examples of counterfactals for sentiment analysis (top) and natural language model (bottom) respectively" align="center" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Reference</h3><a id="user-content-reference" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Reference" href="#reference"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Matt Gardner, et al. Evaluating Models’ Local Decision Boundaries via Contrast Sets. In Findings of the Association for Computational Linguistics: EMNLP 2020, pages 1307–1323, Online. Association for Computational Linguistics.</p>
<p dir="auto">Pepa Atanasova, et al. Fact Checking with Insufficient Evidence. Transactions of the Association for Computational Linguistics (TACL), 2022.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Manual CF Generation</h2><a id="user-content-manual-cf-generation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Manual CF Generation" href="#manual-cf-generation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/D19-1509.pdf" rel="nofollow">Counterfactual story reasoning and generation</a>,  EMNLP-IJCNLP 2019 (a controversy in overleaf？It is cited in <em>Human annotation</em> and <em>Traditional methods</em> Sections. )</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://openreview.net/pdf?id=Sklgs0NFvr" rel="nofollow">Learning the difference that makes a difference with counterfactually-augmented data</a>,  ICLR 2020</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2020.emnlp-main.12.pdf" rel="nofollow">More bang for your buck: Natural perturbation for robust question answering</a>, EMNLP 2020</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2023.emnlp-main.649.pdf" rel="nofollow">People Make Better Edits: Measuring the Efficacy of LLM-Generated Counterfactually Augmented Data for Harmful Language Detection</a>, EMNLP 2023</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2004.12764.pdf" rel="nofollow">“Call me sexist, but...”: Revisiting Sexism Detection Using Psychological Scales and Adversarial Samples</a>, AAAI 2021</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2020.findings-emnlp.117.pdf" rel="nofollow">Evaluating Models’ Local Decision Boundaries via Contrast Sets</a>, EMNLP finding 2020</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2020.acl-main.499.pdf" rel="nofollow">Logicguided data augmentation and regularization for consistent question answering</a>, ACL 2020.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Automatic CF Generation</h2><a id="user-content-automatic-cf-generation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Automatic CF Generation" href="#automatic-cf-generation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">CF generation studies are relative to language models, such as traditional pre-trained models, e.g., Bert and Roberta, etc., or  large language models, e.g., gpt-3.5 and llama.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Non-prompt based CF Generation</h3><a id="user-content-non-prompt-based-cf-generation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Non-prompt based CF Generation" href="#non-prompt-based-cf-generation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2105.08206" rel="nofollow">LEWIS: Levenshtein editing for unsupervised text style transfer</a> ACL 2021, sentiment transfer</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2020.emnlp-main.699.pdf" rel="nofollow">Unsupervised Text Style Transfer with Padded Masked Language Models</a> EMNLP 2020, sentiment transfer</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2020.acl-main.169.pdf" rel="nofollow">Politeness transfer: A tag and generate approach</a>, ACL 2020, politeness style transfer</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/1804.06437" rel="nofollow">Delete, Retrieve, Generate: A Simple Approach to Sentiment and Style Transfer</a>, NAACL 2018, sentiment transfer: attribution（sentiment-bearing words）  + replacement with retrieval texts</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2012.10040" rel="nofollow">Robustness to Spurious Correlations in Text Classification via Automatically Generated Counterfactuals</a> AAAI 2021, casual score + dictionary replace</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2021.acl-long.26.pdf" rel="nofollow">Exploring the Efficacy of Automatically Generated Counterfactuals for Sentiment Analysis</a>, ACL | IJCNLP 2021, dictionary casual identification + MLM replacement + SVM filter + Moverscore selection.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2020.acl-main.442.pdf" rel="nofollow">Beyond Accuracy: Behavioral Testing of NLP Models with CheckList</a> 2020 ACL, template + dictionary generation</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/1904.01130" rel="nofollow">Paws: Paraphrase adversaries from word scrambling</a>, NAACL 2019, parser template + generation</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2010.08580" rel="nofollow">Linguistically-informed transformations (LIT): A method for automatically generating contrast sets</a> ACL 2020, parser+generation</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2021.acl-long.523.pdf" rel="nofollow">Polyjuice: Generating Counterfactuals for Explaining, Evaluating, and Improving Models</a>, ACL 2021, template + generation</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2107.07150" rel="nofollow">Tailor: Generating and Perturbing Text with Semantic Controls</a>, ACL 2022, parser+generation</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2211.00369v2" rel="nofollow">A general search-based framework for generating textual counterfactual explanations</a>, AAAI 2024, search-based optimization: iterative mask-fill</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2010.12512" rel="nofollow">Generating Plausible Counterfactual Explanations for Deep Transformers in Financial Text Classification</a>, Coling (CCFB) 2020, iterative mask-fill</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.semanticscholar.org/paper/Explaining-Data-Driven-Document-Classifications-Martens-Provost/add9930a368c1f281a1428d09ba65751edf06555" rel="nofollow">Explaining Data-Driven Document Classifications</a>, MIS Quarterly 2014, search-based rationals identification and delete</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/1912.01819" rel="nofollow">Counterfactual Explanation Algorithms for Behavioral and Textual Data</a>, ADAC (CCF None) 2019, attribution features delete.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://cdn.aaai.org/ojs/17594/17594-13-21088-1-2-20210518.pdf" rel="nofollow">Generate Your Counterfactuals: Towards Controlled Counterfactual Generation for Text</a>,  AAAI 2021,  steer internal states</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2021.findings-emnlp.306.pdf" rel="nofollow">Generating Realistic Natural Language Counterfactuals</a>,  EMNLP finding 2021, find perturbation in latent space</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2021.findings-acl.336.pdf" rel="nofollow">Explaining NLP Models via Minimal Contrastive Editing (MiCE)</a>, ACL finding 2021,  attribution + generation</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2022.emnlp-main.484.pdf" rel="nofollow">Let the CAT out of the bag: Contrastive Attributed explanations for Text</a>. EMNLP 2022, attribution + generation</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://dl.acm.org/doi/10.1145/3583780.3615029" rel="nofollow">Relevance-based Infilling for Natural Language Counterfactuals</a> CKLM 2023, improved version of MiCE</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2021.acl-long.196.pdf" rel="nofollow">Kace-Generating Knowledge-Aware Contrastive Explanations for Natural Language Inference</a>,  ACL 2021, rationals + controllable LM</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2305.17075" rel="nofollow">CREST: A Joint Framework for Rationalization and Counterfactual Text Generation</a>, ACL 2023, rationals mask + fill</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2022.findings-emnlp.371.pdf" rel="nofollow">NeuroCounterfactuals: Beyond Minimal-Edit Counterfactuals for Richer Data Augmentation</a>,  EMNLP finding 2022, concept + CLM</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2008.01897.pdf" rel="nofollow">Counterfactual Explanation Based on Gradual Construction for Deep Networks</a> PR 2022, CCFB, mask-infill: important features and CLM fill.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2022.findings-emnlp.170.pdf" rel="nofollow">AutoCAD: Automatically Generate Counterfactuals for Mitigating Shortcut Learning</a> EMNLP finding 2022, mask-infill: attribution and CLM fill</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2021.findings-acl.110.pdf" rel="nofollow">Controlling Text Edition by Changing Answers of Specific Questions</a>, ACL-IJCNLP finding 2021, related word mask and LSTM fill.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2022.acl-long.117.pdf" rel="nofollow">Retrieval-guided Counterfactual Generation for QA</a>, ACL 2022, retrivel context + open-generation</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2022.tacl-1.7.pdf" rel="nofollow">Break, Perturb, Build: Automatic Perturbation of Reasoning Paths Through Question Decomposition</a>, TACL 2022, perturbation + open-generation</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2021.emnlp-main.565.pdf" rel="nofollow">Entity-based knowledge conflicts in question answering</a>, EMNLP 2021, retrivel context + entity-based Substitutions</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2023.emnlp-main.826.pdf" rel="nofollow">EXPLAIN, EDIT, GENERATE: Rationale-sensitive counterfactual data augmentation for multi-hop fact verification</a>, EMNLP 2023, casual modeling generation： rationals + open-generation</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2402.15309" rel="nofollow">Counterfactual generation with identifiability guarantees</a>, NeurIPS 2023, casual modeling generation: sentiment style transfer</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2201.09119" rel="nofollow">A causal lens for controllable text generation</a>, NeurIPS 2021, casual modeling generation: text attribution transfer</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2305.13535.pdf" rel="nofollow">Improving Classifier Robustness through Active Generation of Pairwise Counterfactuals</a>, EMNLP finding 2023, a strategy observing a more robust CF Labeler.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Prompt based CF Generation</h3><a id="user-content-prompt-based-cf-generation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Prompt based CF Generation" href="#prompt-based-cf-generation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2309.13340v1.pdf" rel="nofollow">Llms as counterfactual explanation modules: Can chatgpt explain black-box text classifiers?</a>, AAAI 2024(update url, Todo)</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2023.acl-long.302.pdf" rel="nofollow">DISCO: Distilling Counterfactuals with Large Language Models</a>,  ACL 2023</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2310.00603v2.pdf" rel="nofollow">Faithful Explanations of Black-box NLP Models Using LLM-generated Counterfactuals</a>, ICLR 2024</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://aclanthology.org/2024.eacl-long.113.pdf" rel="nofollow">CATfOOD: Counterfactual Augmented Training for Improving Out-of-Domain Performance and Calibration</a>, EACL 2024</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2311.08648.pdf" rel="nofollow">Explore Spurious Correlations at the Concept Level in Language Models for Text Classification</a> arxive 2023 ( Undo in overleaf: Detect the spurious correlation between concept and label, and simply propose to use cfs to alleviate spurious.)</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2306.11260.pdf" rel="nofollow">A Novel Counterfactual Data Augmentation Method for Aspect-Based Sentiment Analysis</a>, ACML 2023</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2210.04873.pdf" rel="nofollow">CORE: A Retrieve-then-Edit Framework for Counterfactual Data Generation</a>, EMNLP finding 2022</p>
